Im pretty surprise by how big the store is when I went inside. This is a one stop shop for me since they have everything I need or can think of. The stuff I buy there are pretty good quality for the price I pay. the man that work there is very helpful, he help me find the item I need by listen to my description. I live in the neighborhood and whenever I need to buy tools to fix my bike, sink, bathroom, etc. the man that work there always provide helpful suggestion that lead me to the right direction. <Review>The restaurant is beautiful and intimate. The seats are couch cushions and oh so comfortable. We were greeted with a good start of cucumber water and a delicious bread basket. I ordered a glass of Prosecco and my guy ordered a beer. They were out of Blue Moon, so the server came out with a suggested replacement. I thought that was a nice touch rather than just saying "we're out" and leaving it at that.

I ordered the avocado tempura (plated as three wedges), which was as delicious as it sounds. You need to eat all components of this dish not just the fried avocado on its own to really enjoy it to its fullest. I I also ordered the mac 'n cheese, which was decadent, and my guy ordered the chicken and waffles, which were delicious and beautifully plated. We ended the meal by splitting the S'more dessert, scrumptious.

The food was a good portion for me since I am prone to eating smaller bites, but it left my guy hungry a few hours later. I do agree with some of the reviews regarding pricing. It is rather expensive for the amount of food you receive, and would not be my choice for a full meal as the menu itself is a bit limited, but rather for cocktails and maybe an appetizer or two.

Note: I also tried the lemongrass vodka cocktail later on the rooftop, which I highly recommend!< /Review>< pictures>

<user_id>109966883111792284355< /user_id><username>russ sweetser< /username><date>1364575429090</date><rating>4<//rating>< review>
This place is right on the closest corner of commercial activity to my new California residence, so I figured we should probably try it out as soon as possible and branch out from there. My Thai food experience is someone limited to one restaurant back East that everyone proclaimed to be "the best" (and I wholeheartedly agree that it is some of the tastiest pad thai I've had in my 34 years), so I may be a harsh judge of character.
You know when you're a kid and you go to your friends house and their mom makes mac n cheese and its nothing like your mom's mac n cheese? The cheese is different, the macaroni is big and fat and your mom's is lean, the creaminess is all off? That's kind of how I felt about this. Granted, there's definitely more than one way to pad a thai, so I will keep an open mind, but I like my mom's mac n cheese better.
To be fair, we got takeout. The decor inside was very awesome, the staff was extremely pleasant, and the portions were huuuge. So they have that going for them. I intend to return, and branch out of my Thai comfort zone at least twice with this place. Gotta support the guy on the corner for a little bit, amirite guys?</review>

<rating>5</rating>< text>
The custom work this shop is capable of is beyond compare.  There are many examples, so I'll list a few:

1) A new steel frame extensively modified for Di2 electronic shifting and powder-coated for a very reasonable price.
2) A half-dozen wheels built or repaired here, by master wheel builder Tahn, including three dynamo equipped front wheels, a 650B wheel with a Di2 11-speed hub, a set of Derby carbon 26" wheels, and repairs of underbuilt Specialized Roval wheels that keep snapping spokes.  You won't find a better wheel anywhere, carbon or alloy.
3) Three complete frame swaps (all parts transferred from one bike to another.)
4) A Surly front rack modified to have a porteur-rack platform and powder coated.

Silva Cycles is also one of the only places you can get SON (AKA, SON Schmidt) dynamo hubs, Gilles Berthoud bags, Honjo Fenders, Road Runner bags, Compass Tires. and Rivendell bicycles.<//text>

< text>
The *best* Bay Area bike shop. I've known Tony and Tanh for several years and they are masters of their craft.

I moved away from the area and visited several other shops that were "highly rated" on Yelp. Hah, Yelp. That was a mistake. I now make the 60 mile drive to Silva because I wouldn't trust my vintage Dutch frames to anyone else.

Tanh is the man for frame alignment / repair, custom wheels, and obscure configurations. Tony has an uncanny knack for finding the best components and can get anything you need. Lastly, most of their shop is dedicated to frame building and fabrication, not tight spandex shorts and $20,000 carbon fiber yuppie cruisers, which is a good sign.

In short, Silva has always exceeded my expectations, and they're the only shop I frequent.</text>

I cannot say enough good things about Dr. Raza and his staff.

After going to a different place within my husband's Military Concordia network they quoted me roughly 7.5 grand for various dental work. We simply could not afford that with our new house and growing family. This bill was also accompanied by unprofessionalism, high pressure sales tactics and huge wait time.

After seeing his good reviews online we wanted to get a second opinion and see if I needed all that work to begin with (I..uh did, my bad). However the entire experience was a complete opposite. Newer machine made my X-ray's easy. The staff was kind and knowledgeable and I was seen to promptly. After getting a thorough check up they gave me a projected bill. ONE THIRD of what the other place wanted. They offered various payment plans and had very flexible dates for procedures

I just finished a root canal and fillings. I barely felt anything during or after the procedure. The staff and Dr.Raza were so gentle and reassuring. Explaining anything I wanted to know ahead of time, and checked in with me during. I have more dental work to complete including getting wisdom teeth removed. I have full confidence in getting quality work done and plan on taking my twins here for their first dental check up.<//Review>

<Review>In previous reviews, I have complimented Dr. Raza and his fabulous team relating to their professionalism, office cleanliness, compassion for patient care (this is real and in no-way contrived), and also their connections to a much larger network of dental/oral specialist, on and on...  With my latest visit, I have two additional comments that go well beyond all my previous accolades.

1.	This particular assessment speaks directly to Dr. Raza's impeccable integrity and high standards:  During my latest visit, I came into the office in-order to get a  final (permanent-fit) for two new crowns, one of the crowns didn't have a "perfect fit" - what this means is that this particular crown didn't establish a 100% seal around the base tooth.   Dr. Raza was not willing to "settle" with this - he re-ordered another crown and set me up with another appointment, all to get things done RIGHT (at no extra cost to me).  This issue could have been pasted-off as "good-enough" and I would've never been the wiser for it.  If he had "settled" I probably would have been right back in the dental chair - getting this same crown re-done in 3-5 years.  Oh by the way, I have had that "good-enough" kind of work done on me in other offices.  Dr. Raza's work-ethics are truly second to none!

2.	As most of us know; dealing with dental insurance companies isn't the easiest thing to do, many of the insurance policies are written like legal contracts (you almost have to be a lawyer to fully understand these policies)  Now that I'm in my "open season", I've decided to change my insurance coverage.  Dr. Raza's Dental Assistant/Administrator (Ashley) went above and beyond - providing me with key-knowledge and also ensured that I understood the typical short-falls of some insurance policies.   Thanks to Ashley, I believe that I have found the "right" policy for me - going into 2018.< /Review>< Rate>
